-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1d379ccc0eef44aaac8ca9a812d6f66c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1d379ccc0eef44aaac8ca9a812d6f66c");'><span id='1d379ccc0eef44aaac8ca9a812d6f66c_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=651&endYear=651')">651年</a>　入京应举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=652&endYear=652')">652年</a>　在长安参选.本年冬或明年春,作《长安古意》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷2第85页。）</span><div id='poem_11578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长安古意</a><span class='authorDate'>（652年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11578")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_11578_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_11578'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1010, "poem_allusion_11578")'>灌夫</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9677, "poem_allusion_11578")'>子云居</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10009, "poem_allusion_11578")'>鹦鹉杯</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_11578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11578'>长安大道连狭斜，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_11578", 11578, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>青牛</span>白马七香车。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11578'>玉辇纵横过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_11578", 11578, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>主第</span>，金鞭络绎向侯家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11578'>龙衔宝盖承朝日，凤吐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11578", 11578, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>流苏</span>带<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11578", 11578, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>晚霞</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11578'>百丈游丝争绕树，一群娇鸟共啼花。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11578'>啼花戏蝶千门侧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_11578", 11578, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>碧树</span>银台万种色。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11578'>复道<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_11578", 11578, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>交窗</span>作合欢，双阙连甍垂凤翼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11578'>梁家画阁天中起，汉帝金茎云外直。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11578'>楼前相望不相知，陌上相逢讵相识。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11578'>借问吹箫向紫烟，曾经学舞度芳年。<div id='poem_sentence_8_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_11578'>得成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_11578", 11578, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>比目</span>何辞死，愿作鸳鸯不羡仙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_11578'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_11578", 11578, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>比目</span>鸳鸯真可羡，双去双来君不见。<div id='poem_sentence_10_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_11578'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_11578", 11578, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>生憎</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_11578", 11578, "Clauses/22/Comments/1")'>帐额</span>绣孤鸾，好取门帘帖双燕。<div id='poem_sentence_11_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_11578'>双燕双飞绕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_11578", 11578, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>画梁</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_11578", 11578, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>罗帏</span>翠被<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_11578", 11578, "Clauses/25/Comments/1")'>郁金香</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_11578'>片片<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_11578", 11578, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>行云</span>著蝉鬓，纤纤初月上鸦黄。<div id='poem_sentence_13_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_11578'>鸦黄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_11578", 11578, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>粉白</span>车中出，含娇含态情非一。<div id='poem_sentence_14_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_11578'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_11578", 11578, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>妖童</span>宝马<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_11578", 11578, "Clauses/30/Comments/1")'>铁连钱</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_11578", 11578, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>娼妇</span>盘龙金屈膝。<div id='poem_sentence_15_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_11578'>御史府中乌夜啼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1010, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>翠幰</span>没金堤。<div id='poem_sentence_17_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_11578'>挟弹飞鹰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_11578", 11578, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>芙蓉剑</span>，共宿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_11578", 11578, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>娼家</span>日暮紫罗裙，清歌一啭口氛氲。<div id='poem_sentence_20_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_11578'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_11578", 11578, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>北堂</span>夜夜人如月，南陌朝朝骑似云。<div id='poem_sentence_21_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_11578'>南陌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_11578", 11578, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>北堂</span>连北里，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_11578", 11578, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>五剧</span>三条控三市。<div id='poem_sentence_22_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_11578'>弱柳青槐拂地垂，佳气红尘暗天起。<div id='poem_sentence_23_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_11578'>汉代金吾千骑来，翡翠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_11578", 11578, "Clauses/49/Comments/1")'>屠苏</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(10009, "poem_sentence_24_11578")'>鹦鹉杯</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_24_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_11578'>罗襦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_11578", 11578, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>宝带</span>为君解，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_11578", 11578, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>燕歌赵舞</span>为君开。<div id='poem_sentence_25_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_11578'>别有豪华称将相，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_11578", 11578, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>转日回天</span>不相让。<div id='poem_sentence_26_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_11578'>意气由来排<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3577, "poem_sentence_27_11578")'>灌夫</span>，专权判不容萧相。<div id='poem_sentence_27_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_11578'>专权意气本豪雄，青虬紫燕坐春<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作生）</span>风。<div id='poem_sentence_28_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_11578'>自言歌舞长千载，自谓骄奢凌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_11578", 11578, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>五公</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_29_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_11578'>节物风光不相待，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_11578", 11578, "Clauses/61/Comments/1")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1153, "poem_sentence_30_11578")'>桑田</span>碧海</span>须臾改。<div id='poem_sentence_30_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_11578'>昔时金阶白玉堂，即今唯见青松在。<div id='poem_sentence_31_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_11578'>寂寂寥寥扬子居，年年岁岁一床书。<div id='poem_sentence_32_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_11578'>独有南山桂花发，飞来飞去<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_11578", 11578, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>袭人</span>裾。<div id='poem_sentence_33_11578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_11578'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=662&endYear=662')">662年</a>，29岁</div><div id='005f1848a310417d9f0205aaa2f010e4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=662&endYear=662')">662年3月</a>　春末,由河西返回京师。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a49e66fc0a0443d397859db61d6baa18_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a49e66fc0a0443d397859db61d6baa18");'><span id='a49e66fc0a0443d397859db61d6baa18_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=669')">668-669年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='a49e66fc0a0443d397859db61d6baa18' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年4月</a>　四月,至京.为玉京观道士郑大量撰碑。作品：《郑太子碑铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷8第494页。）</span><div id='poem_1363881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郑太子碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（668年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363881")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363881'>若夫苍精授邑。载杓西邻之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363881_comment'></div>赤鸟告祥。方崇北面之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363881_comment'></div>海内奔波。三分与二分交竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363881_comment'></div>寰中同会。七百与八百相符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363881_comment'></div>故能安地轴之倾轮。补乾弦之落紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363881_comment'></div>如砥平道。诸侯遵卜洛之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363881_comment'></div>似石磐基。宗子绍维城之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363881_comment'></div>大矣哉周之有天下也。年将庆远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363881_comment'></div>叶带枝繁。郑国桓公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363881_comment'></div>宣王母弟。水双河济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363881_comment'></div>泄云雨以开封。皋二成平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363881_comment'></div>连古今而锡类。犬牙晋楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363881_comment'></div>鼎定齐秦。时遇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1363881", 1363881, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>斗蛇</span>之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363881_comment'></div>乍进牵羊之弊。虽地承负黍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363881_comment'></div>国祚弥而无穷。天锡香兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363881_comment'></div>家风邵为逾远。太子寿者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363881_comment'></div>康公之子。桓公之二十代孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363881_comment'></div>聪明神智。晖映当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363881_comment'></div>涯涘清深。指鳖川而激量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363881_comment'></div>圭璋特达。与龙辂而齐光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363881_comment'></div>因以运逢阳城。败我郑次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363881_comment'></div>辛亥之岁。崩山荡岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363881_comment'></div>馁锐气于韩兵。降志辱身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363881_comment'></div>钦盟符于晋血。邑封千户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363881_comment'></div>官具百僚。今之寿城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363881_comment'></div>斯其地也。享年七十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363881_comment'></div>薨于晋。葬于天陵南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363881_comment'></div>灵原超忽。永深埋玉之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363881_comment'></div>荒陇凄其。谁识生金之字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363881_comment'></div>玉京观道士郑大量家长郑君。则合宗并太子之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363881_comment'></div>胜业孤扬。清晖竞远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363881_comment'></div>逍遥林外。放旷烟霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363881_comment'></div>凝皓素于黄庭。养神气于元宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363881_comment'></div>以为霓旌扬汉。犹寻朽骨之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363881_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1363881", 1363881, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>鹤驾</span>停空。尚谒先人之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363881_comment'></div>于是芟荒薙蔓。徙植延阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363881_comment'></div>丰碑下鹿卢。高坟疏马鬣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363881_comment'></div>得青乌之旧地。临绛邑之新田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363881_comment'></div>于是大唐总章元年岁次戊辰五月甲申之一日也。尔其表里山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363881_comment'></div>极目原野。九京以送其往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1363881_comment'></div>二水以流其恶。山岩霜雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1363881_comment'></div>邀处子以同嬉。奋衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1363881_comment'></div>似群仙而共远。窥晋臣于泉路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363881_comment'></div>依希夏日之光。思汉帝于云衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363881_comment'></div>髣髴秋风之咏。虽复相望绝代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363881_comment'></div>固可气类同年。岂使素烈景风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363881_comment'></div>清猷澹味。金石之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1363881_comment'></div>堙灭而无闻乎。故式绍前范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1363881_comment'></div>传之永代。将日月以居诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1363881_comment'></div>邈宇宙而长久。词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1363881_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1363881'>周封懿族。郑国开疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1363881_comment'></div>始连高华。终带崇芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1363881_comment'></div>东西橘徙。人物绛乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1363881_comment'></div>萧条河曲。凭𨌎荣阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1363881_comment'></div>戎马生郊。兵车乱辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1363881_comment'></div>众雄相竞。郡公未绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1363881_comment'></div>烟尘四起。纵横四结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1363881_comment'></div>园寝成泣。偪阳成血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1363881_comment'></div>家声已溃。出质而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1363881_comment'></div>西光未谢。东府行开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1363881_comment'></div>乡关寂寞。城邑徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1363881_comment'></div>三乡二鄙。风月池台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1363881_comment'></div>广阳已失。年其不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1363881_comment'></div>魄散东山。魂归北郏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1363881_comment'></div>披榛卜葬。分晋献绛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1363881_comment'></div>露泫仍泣。云屯即愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1363881_comment'></div>川源遽徙。居处不留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1363881_comment'></div>源既号灵。城犹名寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1363881_comment'></div>摧残剪树。零落为邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1363881_comment'></div>碑失黄砻。铭摧白楸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1363881_comment'></div>猗欤积善。克昌后孕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1363881_comment'></div>丹灶九飞。清溪千仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1363881_comment'></div>眷兹幽陇。清风丕振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1363881_comment'></div>勒石扬声。闻之陈信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1363881_comment'></div>左右原野。表里山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1363881_comment'></div>析城<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1363881", 1363881, "Clauses/150/Comments/0")'>王屋</span>。汾川帝歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1363881_comment'></div>新城树少。故绛人多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1363881_comment'></div>悠悠万代。见此如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1363881_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1363881_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=668&endYear=668')">668年</a>　在京,有《同崔录事哭郑员外》<span id='poem_sentence_0_11555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11555'>伊人表时彦，飞誉满司存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11560'>敛衽辞丹阙，悬旗<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作津）</span>陟翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11560'>野禽喧戍鼓，春草变征衣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11560'>回顾长安道，关山起夕霏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11560'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_11560_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　处太白山中.本年初,有《首春贻京邑文士》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷3第149页。本年秋,其父丧.据张谱第175页。）</span><div id='poem_11564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>首春贻京邑文士</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11564")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_11564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11564'>寂寂罢将迎，门无车马声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11564'>横琴荅山水，披卷阅公卿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11564'>忽闻岁云晏，倚杖出檐楹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11564'>寒辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_11564", 11564, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>杨柳陌</span>，春满<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作别）</span>凤皇城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11564'>梅花扶院吐，兰叶绕阶生。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11564'>览镜改容色，藏书留姓名。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11564'>时来不假问，生死任交情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11564'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_11564_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　春,居长安,从孙思邈问医。作品：《病梨树赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第26页。孙思邈本隐居于太白山中,此去长安,系由高宗所召,卢照邻为随孙思邈同至长安。）</span><div id='poem_1363857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病梨树赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363857")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363857_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1363857'>癸酉之岁。余卧病于长安光德坊之官舍。父老云。是鄱阳公主之邑司。昔公主未嫁而卒。故其邑废。时有处士孙君思邈居之。君道洽今古。学有数术。高谈正一。则古之蒙庄子。深入不二。则今之维摩诘。及其推步甲子。度量乾坤。飞炼石之奇。洗胃肠之妙。则甘公洛下闳安期先生扁鹊之俦也。自云开皇辛丑岁生。今年九十二矣。询之乡里。咸云数百岁人矣。共语周齐间事。历历如眼见。以此参之。不啻百岁人也。然犹视听不衰。神形甚茂。可谓聪明博达不死者矣。余年垂强仕。则有幽忧之疾。椿菌之性。何其辽哉。于时天子避暑甘泉。邈亦徵诣行在。余独卧病兹邑。阒寂无人。伏枕十旬。闭门三月。庭无众木。惟有病梨一树。围才数握。高仅盈丈。花实憔悴。似不任乎岁寒。枝叶零丁。才有意乎朝暮。嗟乎。同托根于膏壤。俱禀气于太和。而修短不均。荣枯殊质。岂赋命之理。得之自然。将资生之化。有所偏及。树犹如此。人何以堪。有感于怀。赋之云尔。</div><div id='poem_preface_1363857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363857'>天象平运。方祗广植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363857_comment'></div>挺芳桂于月轮。横扶桑于日域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363857_comment'></div>建木耸灵邱之上。蟠桃生巨海之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363857_comment'></div>细叶枝连。洪柯条直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363857_comment'></div>齐天地之一指。任乌兔之栖息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363857_comment'></div>或垂阴万亩。或结子千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363857_comment'></div>何偏施之雨露。何独厚之风烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363857_comment'></div>悯兹珍木。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1363857", 1363857, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>离离</span>幽独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363857_comment'></div>飞茂实于河阳。传芳名于金谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363857_comment'></div>紫涧称其殊旨。元光表其仙族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363857_comment'></div>尔生何为。零丁若斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363857_comment'></div>无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1363857", 1363857, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>轮桷</span>之可用。无栋梁之可施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363857_comment'></div>进无违于斤斧。退无竞于班倕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363857_comment'></div>无庭槐之生意。有岩桐之死枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363857_comment'></div>尔其高才数仞。围仅盈尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363857_comment'></div>修干罕双。枯条每只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363857_comment'></div>叶病多紫。花凋少白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363857_comment'></div>夕鸟怨其巢危。秋蝉悲其翳窄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363857_comment'></div>怯冲飙之摇落。忌炎景之临迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363857_comment'></div>既而地歇蒸雾。天收耀灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363857_comment'></div>西秦明月。东井流星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363857_comment'></div>憔悴孤影。徘徊直形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363857_comment'></div>状金茎之的的。疑石柱之亭亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363857_comment'></div>若夫西海夸父之林。南海蚩尤之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363857_comment'></div>莫不摩霄拂日。藏云吐雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363857_comment'></div>别有桥边朽柱。天上灵楂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363857_comment'></div>年年岁岁。无叶无花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363857_comment'></div>荣辱两齐。吉凶同轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363857_comment'></div>宁守雌以外丧。不修襮而内否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363857_comment'></div>亦犹纵酒高贤。佯狂君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363857_comment'></div>为其吻合。置其忧喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363857_comment'></div>生非我生。物谓之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363857_comment'></div>死非我死。谷神不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363857_comment'></div>混彭殇于一观。庶筌蹄于兹理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363857_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1363857_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=673&endYear=673')">673年</a>　病居长安期间,尚作有《驯鸢赋》、《双槿树赋并序》、《赠许左丞从驾万年宫》等诗文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第8页。）</span>《双槿树赋并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第15页。）</span>《赠许左丞从驾万年宫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第150页。）</span><div id='poem_1363855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>驯鸢赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363855")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363855'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363855'>孕天然之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1363855", 1363855, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>灵质</span>。禀大块之奇工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363855_comment'></div>嘴距足以自卫。毛羽足以淩风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363855_comment'></div>怀九围之远志。托万里之长空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363855_comment'></div>阴云低而含紫。阳星升而带红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363855_comment'></div>经过巫峡之下。惆怅彭门之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363855_comment'></div>既而摧颓短翮。寥落长想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363855_comment'></div>忌蒙庄之见欺。哀武溪之莫往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363855_comment'></div>进谢扶摇之力。退惭归昌之响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363855_comment'></div>腐食多惧。层巢无像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363855_comment'></div>屈猛性以自驯。抱愁容而就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363855_comment'></div>于是傍眺德门。言栖仁路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363855_comment'></div>不践高梁之屋。翔止吾人之树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363855_comment'></div>听鸣鸡于月晓。侣群鹊于星暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363855_comment'></div>狎兰砌之高低。玩荆扉之新故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363855_comment'></div>循广庭之一息。历长檐而径度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363855_comment'></div>若乃风去雨还。河移月落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363855_comment'></div>徘徊乱于双燕。鸣舞均乎独鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363855_comment'></div>乍啸聚于霞庄。时追飞于云阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363855_comment'></div>荷大德之纯粹。将轻姿之陋薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363855_comment'></div>思一报之无阶。欣百龄之有托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363855_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1363855_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1363854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同崔少监作双槿树赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363854")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363854_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1363854'>日昨于著作局见诸著作。竞写双槿树赋。蓬莱山上。即对神仙。芸香阁前。仍观秘宝。金悬秦市。杨子见而无言。纸贵洛城。陆生闻而罢笑。故知柔条朽干。吹嘘变其死生。落叶凋花。剪拂成其光价。方且传石渠之故事。得槿树之新名。足以脂粉仙台。丹青秘府者也。若布衣藜杖。岩栖藿食。当尧时而非吏。处汉代而无田。学涉芜浅。文多瞽陋。宜其屏窜。用其静默。盖穷而思达。人之情也。卑而应高。物之理也。故疾雷作而蛰虫飞。浮云兴而石磶润。不可废也。虽云圣朝多士。而公实居之。草泽有人。亦国家之美事也。故复奖刷刍鄙。作双槿树赋。辞义猥薄。退增惭腼。赋曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1363854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363854'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363854'>方丈蓬莱。邈矣悠哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363854_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>芸扃</span>石室。图天揆日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363854_comment'></div>若乃羲和掌日。太史观星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363854_comment'></div>铜浑玉策。宝笥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>金铭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363854_comment'></div>地则图书之府。人则神仙之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363854_comment'></div>中有芳蕣。郁郁亭亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363854_comment'></div>观其两砌分植。双阶并耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363854_comment'></div>叶镂五衢。荣分四照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363854_comment'></div>纷广庭之靃靡。隐重廊之窈窱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363854_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>青陆</span>至而莺啼。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>朱阳</span>升而花笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363854_comment'></div>紫蒂红蕤。玉蕊苍枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363854_comment'></div>露华的皪。风色徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363854_comment'></div>采粲照灼。婀娜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>隈緌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363854_comment'></div>迫而视之。鸣环动佩歌扇开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363854_comment'></div>远而望之。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>连珠合璧</span>星汉回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363854_comment'></div>状仙人之羽盖。疑佚女之瑶台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363854_comment'></div>寂寞攸利。栖閒此地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363854_comment'></div>委命卷舒。随时荣悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363854_comment'></div>外无婴夭之祸。内有逍遥之致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363854_comment'></div>朝朝暮暮落复开。岁岁年年红以翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363854_comment'></div>若夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1363854", 1363854, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>游蜂戏蝶</span>封其萼。轻烟弱雾络其条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363854_comment'></div>去不谓之损。来不谓之饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363854_comment'></div>故能出君子之殊俗。入诗人之旧谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363854_comment'></div>齐显昧于两曜。效生死于一朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363854_comment'></div>同丧我之非我。固虽凋而不凋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363854_comment'></div>别有亭伯儒门。令思诗友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363854_comment'></div>翰苑旷其吞梦。文锋高而照斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363854_comment'></div>咏芜滋之朝夕。悲积薪之先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363854_comment'></div>缛绣起于缇纺。烟霞生于灌莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363854_comment'></div>岂与岩幽弱筱。涧底枯松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363854_comment'></div>徒冒霜而停雪。空集凤而吟龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363854_comment'></div>讵得奉仙闱之广价。连笔匠之为容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363854_comment'></div>已矣哉。东方生闻而叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363854_comment'></div>故年花落不留人。今年花发非故春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363854_comment'></div>倏兮夕陨。忽兮朝新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363854_comment'></div>侏儒何功兮短饱。曼倩何负兮长贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363854_comment'></div>聊寄辞于庭树。傥有感于平津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363854_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1363854_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠许左丞从驾万年宫</a><span class='authorDate'>（673年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11571")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_11571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11571'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11571'>闻道上之回，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_11571", 11571, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>诏跸</span>下蓬莱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11571'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_11571", 11571, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>中枢</span>移北斗，左辖去南台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11571'>黄山闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11571", 11571, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>凤笛</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作吹）</span>，清跸侍龙媒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11571'>曳日朱旗卷，参云<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_11571", 11571, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>金障</span>开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11571'>朝参五城柳，夕宴柏梁杯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11571'>汉畤光如月，秦祠听似雷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11571'>寂寂芸香阁，离思独悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11571'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_11571_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
武威（凉州）
-----detail

-----title
三台（梓州）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=663&endYear=663')">663年</a>　入蜀,经梓州,逢李荣奉召入京,有《赠李荣道士》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第51页。）</span><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_11572_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_11572'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_0_11572'>锦节衔天使，琼仙驾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_11572", 11572, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>羽君</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11572'>投金翠山曲，奠璧清江濆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11572'>圆洞开<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11572", 11572, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>丹鼎</span>，方坛聚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11572", 11572, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>绛云</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11572'>宝<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作资）</span>贶幽难识，空歌迥易分。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11572'>风摇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_11572", 11572, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>十洲</span>影，日乱九江文。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11572'>敷诚归上帝，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_11572", 11572, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>应诏</span>在明君。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11572'>独有<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(584, "poem_sentence_6_11572")'>南冠</span>客，耿耿泣离群。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11572'>遥看八会所，真气晓氤氲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11572'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_11572_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=663&endYear=663')">663年</a>　在蜀.因事被拘,有《狱中学骚体》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷4第268页。）</span><div id='poem_11591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狱中学骚体</a><span class='authorDate'>（663年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11591")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_11591_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11591'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11591'>夫何秋夜之无情兮，皎皛悠悠而太长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11591'>圜户杳其幽邃兮，愁人披此严霜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11591'>见河汉之西落，闻鸿雁之南翔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11591'>山有桂兮桂有芳，心思君兮君不将。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11591'>忧与忧兮相积，欢与欢兮两忘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11591'>风袅袅兮木纷纷，凋绿叶兮吹白云。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11591'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_11591", 11591, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>寸步千里</span>兮不相闻，思公子兮日将曛。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11591'>林已暮兮鸟群飞，重门掩兮人径稀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11591'>万族皆有所托兮，蹇独淹留而不归。<div id='poem_sentence_8_11591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_11591'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_11591_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=664&endYear=664')">664年</a>　出狱,有《穷鱼赋》,以大鹏鸟救穷鱼的故事,对自身受陷又遇友人搭救的过程做了艺术的表现。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第12页。）</span><div id='poem_1363856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>穷鱼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（664年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363856")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363856_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1363856'>余曾有横事被拘。为群小所使。将致之深议。友人救护得免。窃感赵壹穷鸟之事。遂作穷鱼赋。常思报德。故冠之篇首云。</div><div id='poem_preface_1363856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363856'>有一巨鳞。东海波臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363856_comment'></div>洗净月浦。涵丹锦津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363856_comment'></div>映红莲而得性。戏碧浪以全身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363856_comment'></div>宕而失水。届于阳濒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363856_comment'></div>渔者观焉。乃具竿索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363856_comment'></div>集朋党。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1363856", 1363856, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>凫趋雀跃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363856_comment'></div>风驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1363856", 1363856, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>电往</span>。竞下任公之钓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363856_comment'></div>争陈豫且之网。蝼蚁见而甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363856_comment'></div>猵獭闻而抵掌。于是长舌利嘴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363856_comment'></div>曳纶垂钩。拖鬐挫鬣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363856_comment'></div>抚背扼喉。动摇不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363856_comment'></div>腾跃无由。有怀纤润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363856_comment'></div>宁望洪流。大鹏过而哀之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363856_comment'></div>昔予为鲲也。与是游乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363856_comment'></div>自予羽化。之子其孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363856_comment'></div>俄抚翼而下。负之而趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363856_comment'></div>南浮七泽。东汎五湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363856_comment'></div>是鱼也已相忘于江海。而渔者犹怅望于泥涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363856_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1363856_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=664&endYear=664')">664年</a>　出狱.在蜀中,往来梓州、剑州、利州等地。作品：《送梓州高参军还京》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷2第132页。）</span>《宴梓州南亭诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷6第376页。）</span>《宴梓州南亭得池字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷3第147页。）</span><div id='poem_11543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送梓州高参军还京</a><span class='authorDate'>（664年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11543")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_11543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11543'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11543'>京洛风尘远，褒斜烟露<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作雾）</span>深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11543'>北游君似智，南飞我异禽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11543'>别路琴声断，秋山猿鸟吟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11543'>一乖青岩酌，空伫白云心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11543_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11543'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_11543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1363865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宴梓州南亭诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（664年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363865")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363865'>梓州城池亭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363865_comment'></div>长史张公听讼之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1363865", 1363865, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>别所</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363865_comment'></div>徒观其岩嶂重复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363865_comment'></div>川流灌注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363865_comment'></div>云窗绮阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363865_comment'></div>负绣堞之逶迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363865_comment'></div>涧户山楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363865_comment'></div>带金隍之缭绕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363865_comment'></div>信巴蜀之奇制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363865_comment'></div>时凤扆多閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363865_comment'></div>上得和平之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363865_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1363865", 1363865, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>鳀瀛</span>有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363865_comment'></div>下无交争之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363865_comment'></div>以公寄切上僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363865_comment'></div>故久无州将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363865_comment'></div>连四千石之重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363865_comment'></div>总十万井之雄班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363865_comment'></div>职逾剧而道弥高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363865_comment'></div>位逾崇而德弥广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363865_comment'></div>市狱无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363865_comment'></div>时狎鸟于城隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363865_comment'></div>邦国不空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363865_comment'></div>且观鱼于濠上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363865_comment'></div>宾阶月上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363865_comment'></div>横联蜷之桂枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363865_comment'></div>野院风归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363865_comment'></div>动葳蕤之萱草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363865_comment'></div>则有明珠爱客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363865_comment'></div>置芳酒于十旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363865_comment'></div>羽服神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363865_comment'></div>契仙游于五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363865_comment'></div>圆潭泻镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363865_comment'></div>光浮落日之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363865_comment'></div>杂树开帏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363865_comment'></div>彩缀飞烟之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363865_comment'></div>藤萝杳蔼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363865_comment'></div>挂疏阴以送秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363865_comment'></div>凫雁参差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363865_comment'></div>结流音而将夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363865_comment'></div>百年之欢不再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1363865_comment'></div>千里之会何常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1363865_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1363865", 1363865, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>下客</span>悽惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1363865_comment'></div>暂停归辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363865_comment'></div>高人赏玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363865_comment'></div>岂辍斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363865_comment'></div>咸请赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363865_comment'></div>以纪盛集。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1363865_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11567?labeling=true' "poem_title_11567")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_11567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11567'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_11567", 11567, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>二条</span>开胜迹，大隐叶冲规。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11567'>亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作斋）</span>阁分危岫，楼台绕曲池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11567'>长薄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11567", 11567, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>秋烟</span>起，飞梁古蔓垂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11567'>水鸟翻荷叶，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_11567", 11567, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>山虫</span>咬<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作交）</span>桂枝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11567'>游人惜将晚，公子爱忘疲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11567'>愿得回<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_11567", 11567, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>三舍</span>，琴尊长若斯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11567'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_11567_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
剑阁（临津）
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_2_11518'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_11518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年7月</a>　七月,为益州大都督府长史胡树礼之继母韦夫人作赞。作品：《相乐夫人檀龛赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷7第422页。）</span><div id='poem_1363869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>相乐夫人檀龛赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（666年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363869")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1363869_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1363869'>相乐夫人韦氏者。益州都督长史胡公之继亲也。夫人寓迹兰闺。栖情香岫。琢磨六行。与三明而并驱。驰骛四禅。将十训而齐驾。粤以乾封纪岁。流火司晨。敬遣灵龛。奉图真相。青莲皓月。争华蚊睫之端。宝树天花。竞爽鸿毛之际。纳须弥于纤芥。尝谓徒言。置由旬于方丈。今过其实。重宣此义。敢为赞云。</div><div id='poem_preface_1363869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363869'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363869'>猗欤宝相，显允神功。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1363869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1363869'>规模鹿苑，图写龙宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1363869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1363869'>分身谛听，列坐谈空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1363869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1363869'>群天飒纚，众宝玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1363869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1363869'>雕窗引月，镂网摇风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1363869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1363869'>一窥妙境，高谢尘蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1363869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1363869'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1363869_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=666&endYear=666')">666年</a>　在新都尉任上.为益州长史胡树礼亡女作造画赞。作品：《益州长史胡树礼为亡女造画赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷7第427页。）</span><div id='poem_1363870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>逞妙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363870_comment'></div>徒鏧中人之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363870_comment'></div>架宝崇奢。<div class='inline' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1363870", 1363870, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>穷形尽相</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363870_comment'></div>陋燕壁之含丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363870_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1363870", 1363870, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>写妙</span>分容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363870_comment'></div>嗤吴屏之坠笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363870_comment'></div>式扬显福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363870_comment'></div>俾赞幽魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363870_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363870_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1363870_comment'></div>功超十地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363870_comment'></div>伟欤大士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363870_comment'></div>宏兹远致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363870_comment'></div>追恸幽途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363870_comment'></div>载营檀施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1363870_comment'></div>皎洁霜纨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1363870_comment'></div>照影丹素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1363870_comment'></div>果发金口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1363870_comment'></div>莲生玉步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1363870_comment'></div>地宝天花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1363870_comment'></div>慧炬长设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1363870_comment'></div>迷津永度。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1363870_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=667&endYear=667')">667年</a>　在新都尉任上。作品：《十五夜观灯》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷2第113页。）</span>《文翁讲堂》<span "poem_title_11523")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_11523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11523'><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年</a>，36岁</div><div id='0ec0cfc161e04e118a56d193e8db73ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=669&endYear=669')">669年5月</a>　五月,抵成都,作《对蜀父老问》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷6第387页。）</span><div id='poem_1363879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>对蜀父老问</a><span class='authorDate'>（669年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363879")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363879'>龙集<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>荒落</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363879_comment'></div>律纪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>蕤宾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363879_comment'></div>余自丰镐归于五津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363879_comment'></div>从王事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363879_comment'></div>丁丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363879_comment'></div>届于升仙桥上送客亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363879_comment'></div>即相如所谓不乘高车驷马不出汝下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363879_comment'></div>遇蜀父老皤然庞眉华发者休于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363879_comment'></div>谓余曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363879_comment'></div>子非衣冕之族欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363879_comment'></div>文章之徒欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363879_comment'></div>饰仁义以干时乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363879_comment'></div>怀诗书以邀名乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363879_comment'></div>吾闻诸夫子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363879_comment'></div>邦有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363879_comment'></div>贫且贱焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363879_comment'></div>耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363879_comment'></div>当今万方日照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363879_comment'></div>九有风靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363879_comment'></div>主上垂衣裳正南面而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363879_comment'></div>庸非有道乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363879_comment'></div>而子爵不登<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>上造</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363879_comment'></div>位不至中涓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363879_comment'></div>藜羹不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363879_comment'></div>裋褐不全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363879_comment'></div>庸非贫贱乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363879_comment'></div>吾视子形容憔悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363879_comment'></div>颜色疲怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363879_comment'></div>心若涉六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363879_comment'></div>眼若营四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363879_comment'></div>何其无耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363879_comment'></div>何其不一干圣主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363879_comment'></div>效智出奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363879_comment'></div>何<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>栖栖默默</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363879_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>自苦</span>若斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363879_comment'></div>吾闻克为卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363879_comment'></div>失则烹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363879_comment'></div>何故区区冘冘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363879_comment'></div>无所成名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363879_comment'></div>余笑而应之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1363879_comment'></div>井鱼不可以语于海者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1363879_comment'></div>拘于墟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1363879_comment'></div>夏虫不可以语于冰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363879_comment'></div>笃于时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363879_comment'></div>盖闻智者不背时而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>徼幸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363879_comment'></div>明者不违道以干非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363879_comment'></div>是以圣贤驰骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1363879_comment'></div>莫救三家之辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1363879_comment'></div>匹夫高抗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1363879_comment'></div>不屈万乘之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1363879_comment'></div>道在则箪瓢匪陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1363879_comment'></div>义存则圭组斯违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1363879_comment'></div>或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>立谈</span>以邀鼎食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1363879_comment'></div>或白首而甘布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1363879_comment'></div>或委辂而事属论都之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1363879_comment'></div>或射钩以相遇匡霸之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1363879_comment'></div>亦有朝为伊周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1363879_comment'></div>暮为桀蹠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1363879_comment'></div>当其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1363879_comment'></div>袭珩佩之锵锵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1363879_comment'></div>失其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1363879_comment'></div>委沟渠而喀喀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1363879_comment'></div>故使龙邱先生羞闻拥彗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1363879_comment'></div>雁门太守不知缝掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1363879_comment'></div>孟轲偃蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1363879_comment'></div>为王者师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1363879_comment'></div>范睢匍匐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1363879_comment'></div>为诸侯客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1363879_comment'></div>富贵者君子之馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1363879_comment'></div>仁义者贤达之常迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1363879_comment'></div>来不可违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1363879_comment'></div>类鸿雁之随阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1363879_comment'></div>去不可留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1363879_comment'></div>同白驹之过隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1363879_comment'></div>行苏张之辩于娲燧之年则迂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1363879_comment'></div>用彭韩之术于尧舜之朝则舛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1363879_comment'></div>守夷齐之节于汤武之时则孤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1363879_comment'></div>抱申商之法于成康之日则愚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1363879_comment'></div>彼一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1363879_comment'></div>此一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1363879_comment'></div>易时而处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1363879_comment'></div>失其所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1363879_comment'></div>大唐之有天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1363879_comment'></div>出入三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1363879_comment'></div>五十馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1363879_comment'></div>月竁来庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1363879_comment'></div>风邱款塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1363879_comment'></div>华旌已偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1363879_comment'></div>羽檄已平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1363879_comment'></div>虽有廉白之将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1363879_comment'></div>孙吴之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1363879_comment'></div>百胜无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1363879_comment'></div>千里不留行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1363879_comment'></div>无所用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1363879_comment'></div>社首既禅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1363879_comment'></div>介邱既封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1363879_comment'></div>创明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1363879_comment'></div>立辟雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1363879_comment'></div>虽有阙里之圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1363879_comment'></div>淹中之儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1363879_comment'></div>叔孙通之蕝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1363879_comment'></div>公玉带之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1363879_comment'></div>将焉设也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1363879_comment'></div>咸英并作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1363879_comment'></div>韶武毕用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1363879_comment'></div>奏之方泽而地祇登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1363879_comment'></div>升之圆丘而天神降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1363879_comment'></div>虽有伶伦伯夔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1363879_comment'></div>延陵子期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1363879_comment'></div>操雅曲则风云动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1363879_comment'></div>激悽音则草木悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1363879_comment'></div>又何施也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1363879_comment'></div>画衣莫犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1363879_comment'></div>囹圄不修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1363879_comment'></div>虽有咎繇仲甫之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1363879_comment'></div>释之定国之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1363879_comment'></div>金科在握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1363879_comment'></div>丹笔如流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1363879_comment'></div>非急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1363879_comment'></div>人归东户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1363879_comment'></div>家沐南薰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1363879_comment'></div>山泽无蹊隧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1363879_comment'></div>鸡犬不相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1363879_comment'></div>虽有文翁黄霸之述职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1363879_comment'></div>子游子贱之弦歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1363879_comment'></div>政成礼让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1363879_comment'></div>俗被雍和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1363879_comment'></div>固无取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1363879_comment'></div>干戈已戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1363879_comment'></div>礼乐已兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1363879_comment'></div>刑罚已措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1363879_comment'></div>梁父已升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1363879_comment'></div>公卿常伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1363879_comment'></div>庶政其凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1363879_comment'></div>虽有鸿才大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1363879_comment'></div>丽句<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>丰词</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1363879_comment'></div>发言盈乎百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1363879_comment'></div>濡翰周乎四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1363879_comment'></div>略无益于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1363879_comment'></div>而适足以怫之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1363879_comment'></div>是故天子恭己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1363879_comment'></div>群臣演成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1363879_comment'></div>攘袂而陵稷契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1363879_comment'></div>抚掌而笑阿衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1363879_comment'></div>无为而万物皆遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1363879_comment'></div>不言而品汇咸亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1363879_comment'></div>莫不称赞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1363879", 1363879, "Clauses/146/Comments/0")'>鸿烈</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1363879_comment'></div>揄扬颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1363879_comment'></div>言殊者招累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1363879_comment'></div>行危者相倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1363879_comment'></div>效智者辍谈于草泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1363879_comment'></div>出奇者裹足于山楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1363879_comment'></div>许由去而尧臣不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1363879_comment'></div>善卷逃而舜德不轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1363879_comment'></div>夫周冕虽华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1363879_comment'></div>猿猴不之好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1363879_comment'></div>夏屋虽崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1363879_comment'></div>骐骥不之处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1363879_comment'></div>载鼷以车马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1363879_comment'></div>不如放之于薮穴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1363879_comment'></div>乐鴳以钟鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1363879_comment'></div>不如栖之以深林也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1363879_comment'></div>此数物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1363879_comment'></div>岂恶荣而好辱哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1363879_comment'></div>盖不失其天真也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1363879_comment'></div>若余者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1363879_comment'></div>十五而志于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1363879_comment'></div>四十而无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1363879_comment'></div>咏羲农之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1363879_comment'></div>玩姬孔之篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1363879_comment'></div>周游几万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1363879_comment'></div>驰骋数十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1363879_comment'></div>时复陵霞泛月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1363879_comment'></div>搦札弹弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1363879_comment'></div>随时上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1363879_comment'></div>与俗推迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1363879_comment'></div>门有张公之雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1363879_comment'></div>突无墨子之烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1363879_comment'></div>虽吾道之穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1363879_comment'></div>夫何妨乎浩然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1363879_comment'></div>今将授子以中和之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1363879_comment'></div>申子以封禅之篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1363879_comment'></div>终眇惭乎指地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1363879_comment'></div>窃所慕乎谈天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1363879_comment'></div>于是蜀父老再拜而谢曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1363879_comment'></div>鄙夫瞽陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1363879_comment'></div>长自愚惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1363879_comment'></div>习俗遐陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1363879_comment'></div>不游上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1363879_comment'></div>闻王人之休旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1363879_comment'></div>听皇猷之允塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1363879_comment'></div>亦犹献雉而遇司南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1363879_comment'></div>御龙而光有北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1363879_comment'></div>请终馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1363879_comment'></div>永告邛僰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_194_1363879_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='poem_title_11598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11598'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11598'>一鸟自北燕，飞来向西蜀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11598'>单栖剑门上，独舞岷山足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11598'>昂藏多古貌，哀怨有新曲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11598'>群凤从之游，问之何所欲？<div id='poem_sentence_3_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11598'>荅言寒乡子，飘飖万馀里。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11598'>不息恶木枝，不饮盗泉水。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11598'>常思稻粱遇，愿栖梧桐树。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11598'>智者不我邀，愚夫余不顾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11598'>所以成独立，耿耿岁云暮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_11598'>日夕苦风霜，思归赴洛阳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_11598'>羽翮毛衣短，关山道路长。<div id='poem_sentence_10_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_11598'>明月流客思，白云迷故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_11_11598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_11598'>谁能借风便，一举凌苍苍。<div id='poem_title_11599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠益府裴录事</a><span class='authorDate'>（670年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span
