id='poem_title_11599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11599'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11599'>忽忽岁云暮，相望限风烟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11599'>长歌欲对酒，危坐遂停弦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11599'>停弦变霜露，对酒怀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11599", 11599, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>朋故</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11599'>朝看<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_11599", 11599, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>桂蟾</span>晚，夜闻鸿雁度。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11599'>鸿度何时还，桂晚不同攀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11599'>浮云映丹壑，明月满青山。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11599'>青山<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_11599", 11599, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>云路</span>深，丹壑月华临。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11599'>耿耿离忧积，空令星鬓<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作发）</span>侵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11599'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_11599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年1-2月</a>　在新都尉任上.一、二月间,作《益州至真观主黎君碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷7第432页。）</span><div id='poem_1363880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益州至真观主黎君碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年1-2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363880")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363880'>若夫三清上列。瑶关控日月之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363880_comment'></div>八洞深居。贝阙吐山河之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363880_comment'></div>虽复扶桑大帝。传赤字于东华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363880_comment'></div>安宝神君。受青符于南极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363880_comment'></div>犹未能发挥不宰。复归无物之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363880_comment'></div>开凿妙门。言谢有为之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363880_comment'></div>其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>冯冯翼翼</span>。百姓存焉而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363880_comment'></div>杳杳冥冥。万族死之而无愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363880_comment'></div>独为众化之宗者。其惟元始天尊乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363880_comment'></div>暨乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>蹩蹩</span>为仁。跛跛为义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363880_comment'></div>鸿胪传小儒之具。缄縢为大盗之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363880_comment'></div>尧禹生而天下火驰。姬孔出而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>群方</span>鼎沸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363880_comment'></div>则有氤氲帝祖。发皓鬓于东周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363880_comment'></div>兆朕皇舆。飞紫云于西道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363880_comment'></div>凤交开景。返<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>徐甲</span>之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/29/Comments/1")'>营魂</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363880_comment'></div>龙光照天。杜宣尼之神气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363880_comment'></div>得一吹万。有大造于苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363880_comment'></div>把十蹈五。树灵基于宝祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363880_comment'></div>能使秦皇东指。见赤舄而长怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363880_comment'></div>汉帝北游。望青烟而下拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363880_comment'></div>于是灵山水府。俱为鍊玉之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363880_comment'></div>甲第离宫。多入空歌之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363880_comment'></div>青牛道士。按锦节于中都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363880_comment'></div>白鹿仙人。列瑶坛于八表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363880_comment'></div>乃剑门西拒。邛关南望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363880_comment'></div>星桥对斗。像牛汉之秋横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363880_comment'></div>月硖萦城。疑兔轮之晓落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363880_comment'></div>武骑<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>迁升</span>之路。冠盖云飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363880_comment'></div>文翁讲肄之堂。英灵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>雾聚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363880_comment'></div>岩开菌桂。蕴金碧之祥光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363880_comment'></div>涧吐夭桃。积神仙之粹气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363880_comment'></div>至真观者。隋开皇二年之所立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363880_comment'></div>寻属炀帝骄淫。蜀王奢僭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363880_comment'></div>冕旒多事。有惭七圣之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363880_comment'></div>几杖不朝。未遑八仙之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363880_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>紫台</span>初构。霜露沾衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363880_comment'></div>碧洞新开。蓬莱变海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363880_comment'></div>仙居制度。与云雷而共屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363880_comment'></div>象帝威仪。将市朝而犹梗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363880_comment'></div>皇家缵戎牝谷。乘大道而驱除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1363880_comment'></div>盘根濑乡。拥真人之阀阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1363880_comment'></div>高祖以汾阳如雪。当金阙之上仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1363880_comment'></div>太宗以峒山顺风。属瑶京之下视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363880_comment'></div>武皇帝凝旒紫阁。悬镜丹台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363880_comment'></div>运璇极而正乾坤。坐闿阳而调风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363880_comment'></div>变铜浑于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>九洛</span>。鳞羽登歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363880_comment'></div>鸣玉銮于四清。烟霞变色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1363880_comment'></div>焚符破玺。更闻绳燧之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1363880_comment'></div>剖斗折衡。重睹人伦之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1363880_comment'></div>银书纪岱。登日观以论功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1363880_comment'></div>玉牒封梁。下云邱而校美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1363880_comment'></div>千龄胎化。申以驾羽之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1363880_comment'></div>万岁岩音。献以华封之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1363880_comment'></div>耕田凿井者不知自然。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>鼓腹击壤</span>者不知帝力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1363880_comment'></div>呜呼。岂非道风幽赞之效欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1363880_comment'></div>乃回舆诏跸。亲幸樵谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1363880_comment'></div>奉策老君为太上皇帝。仍令天下诸州各立观一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1363880_comment'></div>于是碧楼三袭。上接虹蜺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1363880_comment'></div>绛阙九成。下交星雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1363880_comment'></div>乘云御气。日夕于关山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1363880_comment'></div>荐璧投金。岁时于岳渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1363880_comment'></div>此观地当极要。任切会昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1363880_comment'></div>南邻覆锦之城。西逼吞珠之界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1363880_comment'></div>使星<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>连注</span>。皇华结辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1363880_comment'></div>既而绿地榛芜。朱宫板荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1363880_comment'></div>非夫位膺金策。名载<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>琼轩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1363880_comment'></div>为紫帝之群宾。列黄庭之上格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1363880_comment'></div>孰能居此。栋梁平圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1363880_comment'></div>丹雘长楼。大开流电之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1363880_comment'></div>广制明霞之宇。观主三洞法师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1363880_comment'></div>姓黎讳某。广汉雒人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1363880_comment'></div>金天命秩。即有天地之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1363880_comment'></div>火正分司。实掌羲和之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1363880_comment'></div>夏殷之际。代为伯相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1363880_comment'></div>或食邑于鲁。或书社于卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1363880_comment'></div>故鲁之黎城。卫之黎阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1363880_comment'></div>即其地也。魏晋之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1363880_comment'></div>或立功于吴。剖符于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1363880_comment'></div>在吴者其后封于寿春。黎将故城有黎氏之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1363880_comment'></div>石文石阙之字在焉。在蜀苻坚时奉为蜀郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1363880_comment'></div>北齐时练山为益州刺史。故子孙因家于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1363880_comment'></div>法师练山之六代孙也。祖宗父泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1363880_comment'></div>并为州郡都主簿平正七职之任。蜀文公之好智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1363880_comment'></div>固让朝恩。秦子整之多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1363880_comment'></div>终从郡辟。礼仪体制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1363880_comment'></div>乡校取式于公曹。狱讼章程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1363880_comment'></div>府主责成于平正。时无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1363880_comment'></div>复闻坐啸之谈。野有让耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1363880_comment'></div>重听行歌之乐。元珠结庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1363880_comment'></div>剖江汉之圆流。紫胞贻祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1363880_comment'></div>动岷精之垂曜。豫章七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1363880_comment'></div>非复常材。朝阳五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1363880_comment'></div>岂云凡鸟。初登小学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1363880_comment'></div>笑孔墨之神劳。一见元书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1363880_comment'></div>以彭聃为已任。玉笈云囊之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1363880_comment'></div>龙缄凤蕴之图。莫不吞楚梦于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1363880_comment'></div>指鲁城于掌上。临长水而饮犊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1363880_comment'></div>不就尧徵。卧巨泽而牧羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1363880_comment'></div>徒劳汉使。冥邱耸驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1363880_comment'></div>左肘符观化之辰。谆壑停装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1363880_comment'></div>横目传栖真之地。贞观之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1363880_comment'></div>有昭庆大法师。魁岸堂堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1363880_comment'></div>威仪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/204/Comments/0")'>肃肃</span>。裂圆冠而焚俗制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1363880_comment'></div>横大帐而抗山谷。声若坻颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1363880_comment'></div>辩均涛发。仲尼河目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1363880_comment'></div>飞电惊人。子贡斗唇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1363880_comment'></div>连环动坐。昂昂不杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1363880_comment'></div>如独鹤之映群鸡。矫矫无双。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1363880_comment'></div>状真龙之对刍狗。于时三蜀耆老咸相谓曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1363880_comment'></div>兴大道者。其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1363880_comment'></div>初袭羽裙。且莅真阳小观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1363880_comment'></div>才麾玉柄。已驰天下大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1363880_comment'></div>寻而广汉士人固请法师为灵集观主。去长桑之故苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1363880_comment'></div>临隐弅之新邱。经之营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1363880_comment'></div>既雕既斲。银台中天而孤出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1363880_comment'></div>珠树匝地而丛生。同赤城之建标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1363880_comment'></div>有黄房之贞构。观中先有天尊真人石像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1363880_comment'></div>大小万馀区。年代寖深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1363880_comment'></div>仪范凋缺。沈沈宝座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1363880_comment'></div>积万古之埃尘。邈邈琼颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1363880_comment'></div>被千龄之苔藓。法师睹斯而流涕曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1363880_comment'></div>不图先圣尊容。零落至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1363880_comment'></div>乃重趼即路。无胈永哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1363880_comment'></div>栉沐几于四时。栖遑周于百舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1363880_comment'></div>誓将崇辑事毕。然后寝食为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1363880_comment'></div>乡曲争持钱物。竞施珍宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1363880_comment'></div>费馀巨万。役不崇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1363880_comment'></div>还开紫翠之容。更表圆明之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1363880_comment'></div>行益州刺史驸马都尉乔君。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>主婿</span>懿亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1363880_comment'></div>勋门盛族。任高方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1363880_comment'></div>寄切西南。法师道叶半千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1363880_comment'></div>神疑正一。而至真福地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1363880_comment'></div>荒凉日久。不有上德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1363880_comment'></div>其谁振之。又表请师为至真观主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1363880_comment'></div>法师升堂慷慨。吐纳元科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1363880_comment'></div>摄齐嘹喨。分明紫诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1363880_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/272/Comments/0")'>词峰</span>云郁。触剑石以飞扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1363880_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_137_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/274/Comments/0")'>义壑</span>泉奔。横玉轮而浩荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1363880_comment'></div>入其门者披烟雾于九天。闻其音者听咸韶于三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1363880_comment'></div>由是户外之履。鱼贯江水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1363880_comment'></div>堂下之宾。鸿行关塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1363880_comment'></div>黄老之学。复于今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1363880_comment'></div>则有王孙之党。都公之伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1363880_comment'></div>名亚春陵。气高韩魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1363880_comment'></div>鹴裘玉剑。散圆庭以陆离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1363880_comment'></div>骥子银鞍。委山衢而沛艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1363880_comment'></div>法师以兹众施。即于天宫后起大讲堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1363880_comment'></div>并造长廊二十馀丈。琳堂郁其峙起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1363880_comment'></div>星闱忽以环周。仰䆗窱以嶙峋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1363880_comment'></div>下峥嵘以广朗。阴娥假道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1363880_comment'></div>窥玉女于南轩。阳乌回辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1363880_comment'></div>炤青禽于北阁。又于观内铸铜钟一口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1363880_comment'></div>重七十斤。立石坛三级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1363880_comment'></div>周回一百步。悬黍玑于碧落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1363880_comment'></div>明月流光。建琼乳于元都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1363880_comment'></div>飞霜蓄韵。坛开锦砌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1363880_comment'></div>类江浦之澄霞。庭列瑶阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1363880_comment'></div>疑昆邱之积雪。每至三辰法会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1363880_comment'></div>八景真游。霓裳荡耀魄之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1363880_comment'></div>羽盖转<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_159_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/318/Comments/0")'>风云</span>之路。通天亘景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1363880_comment'></div>兼造化之全模。带鸟衔虹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1363880_comment'></div>连飞动之奇势。可谓德光而功济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1363880_comment'></div>道胜而名扬者也。前长史范阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1363880_comment'></div>一代羽仪。门倾四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1363880_comment'></div>前长史谯国公。两朝肺腑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1363880_comment'></div>威动百城。并屈银黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1363880_comment'></div>俱伸元素。法师雍容坐镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1363880_comment'></div>啸傲行藏。虽郭先生之礼峻晋侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1363880_comment'></div>蒙庄子之身轻梁相。不能尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1363880_comment'></div>若夫言出于口。龙骥所不能追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1363880_comment'></div>行成于心。王公所不能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1363880_comment'></div>悲怀徇物。风雨晦而逾勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1363880_comment'></div>苦节横秋。冰霜急而逾固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1363880_comment'></div>户居环堵。而岁计有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1363880_comment'></div>道周稊稗。而日用无竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1363880_comment'></div>又于学射灵山别立仙居一所。即至真之珠庭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1363880_comment'></div>栽松莳柏。与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_176_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/353/Comments/0")'>月树</span>而交轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1363880_comment'></div>刻角雕甍。共星楼而接翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1363880_comment'></div>苍郊却倚。犹太行之北登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1363880_comment'></div>锦肆前通。似灞陵之南望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1363880_comment'></div>华表千年之鹤。未见成都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1363880_comment'></div>津亭八月之龙。时归乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1363880_comment'></div>法师出家入道。三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1363880_comment'></div>弟子所得儭施。不可称量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1363880_comment'></div>尽入修营。咸供众用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1363880_comment'></div>见诸疾苦。便开五色之囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1363880_comment'></div>遇彼饥寒。辄有千金之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1363880_comment'></div>巾拂之外。馀无所留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1363880_comment'></div>凡所经过。洪济多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1363880_comment'></div>法师又于咸亨二年正月十八日寝疾之际。闻空中有声曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1363880_comment'></div>天上今欲相烦为玉京观主。法师辞以至真功德未就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1363880_comment'></div>固请不得行。少选之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1363880_comment'></div>所疾便愈。左右侍者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1363880_comment'></div>无不同闻。自是远近道俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1363880_comment'></div>咸共惊嗟。曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1363880_comment'></div>天上知余不肖。将弃余矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1363880_comment'></div>上座<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_196_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/392/Comments/0")'>监斋</span>某等。并回流左映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1363880_comment'></div>策<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_197_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/394/Comments/0")'>地景</span>于丹田。浩气中升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1363880_comment'></div>养天倪于紫室。虽复同班玉籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1363880_comment'></div>并列仙宫。每屈宗师之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1363880_comment'></div>仍修弟子之敬。亦犹披衣齧缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1363880_comment'></div>同德而相尊。云将鸿濛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1363880_comment'></div>比肩而相下。大弟子并仙庭十哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1363880_comment'></div>道家童师。闭门鍊火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1363880_comment'></div>陪啸父之高烟。卜肆驱筠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1363880_comment'></div>记壶公之远御。咸用辑琼台之坠典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1363880_comment'></div>正搴树之颓风。散在人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1363880_comment'></div>敷扬道教。可谓庚桑畏垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1363880_comment'></div>致大壤以匡时。范相鸱夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1363880_comment'></div>行计然而济俗。佥曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1363880_comment'></div>吾师也。整万物而不以为义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1363880_comment'></div>利万代而不以为仁。逍遥乎有无之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1363880_comment'></div>仿偟乎尘垢之外。东郭顺子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1363880_comment'></div>无择存而不论。伯昏瞀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1363880_comment'></div>御寇论而不议。岂使为山九仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1363880_comment'></div>道不列于珠庭。筑馆三休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1363880_comment'></div>功未书于瑶版。下官迷方看博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1363880_comment'></div>邀赤斧于禺山。失路乘槎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1363880_comment'></div>问君平于蜀郡。汾阳处子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1363880_comment'></div>目击而言忘。汉阴丈人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1363880_comment'></div>德全而机谢。是用搜奇井络。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1363880_comment'></div>题片石于灵邱。观艺协晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1363880_comment'></div>见乘云之飞将。苍苍中野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1363880_comment'></div>同销<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_223_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/446/Comments/0")'>地媪</span>之魂。眇眇太初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1363880_comment'></div>独昧天师之化。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_225_1363880'>象帝之先。其谁之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1363880_comment'></div>徒观其妙。莫究其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1363880_comment'></div>果而勿代。为而不恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1363880_comment'></div>强为之名。谓之道纪<span class='inlineComment2'>（其一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_229_1363880'>太朴云季。孝慈已彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1363880_comment'></div>邈邈帝祖。绳绳帝乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1363880_comment'></div>曰神曰圣。为龙为光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1363880_comment'></div>千年受箓。万古称王<span class='inlineComment2'>（其二）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_233_1363880'>于铄帝唐。丕承天秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1363880_comment'></div>道风吹万。元猷配一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1363880_comment'></div>五载乘云。三山礼日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1363880_comment'></div>荐璧延士。投金访术<span class='inlineComment2'>（其三）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_237_1363880'>地分舆井。城连剑阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1363880_comment'></div>锦濑开霞。嵋峰吐月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1363880_comment'></div>白云舒卷。青山回没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1363880_comment'></div>菌阁香飞。桃源花发<span class='inlineComment2'>（其四）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_241_1363880'>紫宸高映。丹宫洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1363880_comment'></div>岩舒金碧。地起楼台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1363880_comment'></div>鹤飞龙度。鸾歌凤回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1363880_comment'></div>星雨交接。风烟去来<span class='inlineComment2'>（其五）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_245_1363880'>宝龟涵影。玉颜乃眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1363880_comment'></div>神剑九光。华冠万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1363880_comment'></div>日轩朝敞。云歌夕转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1363880_comment'></div>紫树琼钟。元坛竹院<span class='inlineComment2'>（其六）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_249_1363880'>伟与上士。昭哉至人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1363880_comment'></div>笙簧道德。粉泽人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1363880_comment'></div>汾阳处子。箕山外臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1363880_comment'></div>遂荒白屋。奄有元津<span class='inlineComment2'>（其七）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_253_1363880'>玉扃将坠。金阶无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1363880_comment'></div>草滋红壁。苔凝绣柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1363880_comment'></div>式伫贤才。崇其彟矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1363880_comment'></div>福庭霞焕。仙徒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_256_1363880", 1363880, "Clauses/513/Comments/1")'>雾聚</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（其八）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_257_1363880'>缥缈四真。雍容十哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1363880_comment'></div>俱升紫宇。并邀清节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1363880_comment'></div>松子排烟。焦君卧雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1363880_comment'></div>辨云悬宇。神游朗彻<span class='inlineComment2'>（其九）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1363880_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_261_1363880'>玉垒庭绅。珠乡胜践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1363880_comment'></div>钟鼎纷蔼。江山悠缅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1363880_comment'></div>薛县池平。莱州水浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1363880_comment'></div>悬日月于鳌极。播天人于凤椽<span class='inlineComment2'>（其十）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1363880_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_265_1363880_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=671&endYear=671')">671年6;7月</a>　夏秋离蜀,北归京洛.行前,有《于时春也,慨然有江湖之思,寄此赠柳九陇》、《还京赠别》等诗。作品：《于时春也慨然有江湖之思寄此赠柳九陇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷1第64页。）</span>《还京赠别》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷2第126页。）</span><div id='poem_11576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>于时春也慨然有江湖之思寄赠柳九陇</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年6;7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11576")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_11576_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_11576'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1683, "poem_allusion_11576")'>彭泽宰</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_11576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11576'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11576'>提琴一万里，负书三十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11576'>晨攀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_11576", 11576, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>偃蹇</span>树，暮宿清泠泉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11576'>翔禽鸣我侧，旅兽过我前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11576'>无人且无事，独酌还独眠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11576'>遥闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5025, "poem_sentence_4_11576")'>彭泽宰</span>，高弄<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3312, "poem_sentence_4_11576")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_11576", 11576, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>武城弦</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11576'>形骸寄文墨，意气托神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11576'>我有壶中要，题为物外篇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11576'>将以贻好道，道远莫致旃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11576'>相思劳日夜，相望阻风烟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_11576'>坐惜春华晚，徒令客思悬。<div id='poem_sentence_9_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_11576'>水去东南地，气凝西北天。<div id='poem_sentence_10_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_11576'>关山悲蜀道，花鸟忆秦川。<div id='poem_sentence_11_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_11576'>天子何时问，公卿本亦<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作不）</span>怜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_11576'>自哀还自乐，归薮复归田。<div id='poem_sentence_13_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_11576'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_11576", 11576, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>海屋</span>银为栋，云车电作鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_14_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_11576'>倘遇鸾将鹤，谁论貂与蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_11576'>莱洲频度浅，桃实几成圆。<div id='poem_sentence_16_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_11576'>寄言<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1683, "poem_sentence_17_11576")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_11576", 11576, "Clauses/34/Comments/1")'>飞凫舄</span></span>，岁晏同<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作共）</span>联翩。<div id='poem_sentence_17_11576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_11576'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_11576_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>还京赠别</a><span class='authorDate'>（671年6;7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11535")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_11535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11535'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11535'>风月清江夜，山水白云朝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11535'>万里同为客，三秋契不凋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11535'>戏凫分断岸，归骑别<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_11535", 11535, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>高标</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11535'>一去仙桥道，还望锦城遥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11535_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11535'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_11535_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
绵阳（巴西）

id='poem_title_1363868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363868'>夫圯上黄公。灵期已远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363868_comment'></div>湘中元乙。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1363868", 1363868, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>化迹</span>难徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363868_comment'></div>况乎神理岿然。近带青溪之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363868_comment'></div>瑰姿可望。俯控丹岩之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363868_comment'></div>予以归骸空谷。言隔市朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363868_comment'></div>濯发长川。载离寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363868_comment'></div>形木双枯。将有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1363868", 1363868, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>终焉之志</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363868_comment'></div>命壶觞而引宴。即沐新兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363868_comment'></div>寻涧户以安歌。仍攀野桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363868_comment'></div>萋萋春草。王孙游兮不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363868_comment'></div>秩秩斯干。幽人去而忘返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363868_comment'></div>鼓我舞我。修袖满于中岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363868_comment'></div>神之听之。多祜兴于触石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363868_comment'></div>爰有嘉命。咸遣赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363868_comment'></div>请题四韵。列之如右。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=674&endYear=674')">674年</a>　客居东龙门山佛寺,服药疗养。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>　客居东龙门山佛寺,服药疗养.有《与洛阳名流朝士乞药直书》一文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷7第414页。）</span><div id='poem_1363859' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363859' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363859?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与洛阳名流朝士乞药直书</a><span class='authorDate'>（675年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363859")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363859'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363859'>幽忧子学道于东龙门山精舍。布衣藜羹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363859_comment'></div>坚卧于一岩之曲。客有过而哀之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363859_comment'></div>青囊中出金花子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1363859", 1363859, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>丹方</span>相遗之。服之病愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363859_comment'></div>视其方。丹砂二斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363859_comment'></div>谷楮子则山中可有。丹砂则渺然难致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363859_comment'></div>昔在关西太白山下。一隐士多元明膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363859_comment'></div>中有丹砂八两。予时居贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363859_comment'></div>不得好上砂。但取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1363859", 1363859, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>马牙</span>颜色微光净者充用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363859_comment'></div>自尔丁府君忧。每一恸哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363859_comment'></div>涕泗中皆药气流出。三四年羸卧苦嗽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363859_comment'></div>几至于不免。复偶于他方中见一说云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363859_comment'></div>丹砂之不精者。服之令人多嗽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363859_comment'></div>访知一处有此物甚佳。两必须钱二千文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363859_comment'></div>则三十二两当取六十四千也。空山卧疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363859_comment'></div>家业先贫。老母年尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363859_comment'></div>兄弟禄薄。若待家办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363859_comment'></div>则委骨于巉岩之峰矣。意者欲以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1363859", 1363859, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>开岁</span>五月谷子熟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363859_comment'></div>试合此药。非天下名流贵族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363859_comment'></div>王公卿士。以仁恻之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363859_comment'></div>达枯骨朽株者。孰能济之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363859_comment'></div>今力疾赋诗一篇。遍呈当代博雅君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363859_comment'></div>虽文不动俗。事或伤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363859_comment'></div>傥遇晏婴。脱左骖而见赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363859_comment'></div>如逢孔子。分秉粟以相忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363859_comment'></div>则越石原宪。不辛苦于当年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363859_comment'></div>惟当坐禅念室。以答深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363859_comment'></div>若诸君子家有好妙砂。能以见及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363859_comment'></div>最为第一。无者各乞一二两药直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363859_comment'></div>是庶几也。仲尼曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363859_comment'></div>有能一日用其力于仁者乎。未有力不足者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363859_comment'></div>又曰。君子无终食之间违仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363859_comment'></div>在坐则参于前。在舆则倚于衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363859_comment'></div>古人心可见矣。又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363859_comment'></div>仁远乎哉。我欲仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363859_comment'></div>斯仁至矣。言能苟行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363859_comment'></div>仁道不远也。朝英贵士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363859_comment'></div>博济而好仁者。何必相识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363859_comment'></div>故知与不知。咸送诗告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363859_comment'></div>请无案剑。同掩体骸云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363859_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1363859_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=675&endYear=675')">675年</a>　客居东龙门山佛寺,服药疗养.有《行路难》（君不见长安城北渭桥边）诗。（君不见长安城北渭桥边）<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷2第80页。）</span><div id='poem_allusion_11583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11583'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11583'>君不见长安城北渭桥边，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_6_11583'>千尺长条百尺枝，月<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作丹）</span>桂星<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作青）</span>榆相蔽亏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_11583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_11583'>珊瑚叶上鸳鸯鸟，凤皇巢里雏鹓儿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11583_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11583'>巢倾枝折凤归去<span id='poem_title_11579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>失群雁</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11579")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_11579_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_11579'>温县明府以雁诗垂示，余以为古之郎官，出宰百里，今之墨绶，入应千官，事止雁行，未宜伤叹。至如羸卧空岩者，乃可为失群恸耳。聊因伏枕多暇，以斯文应之。</div><div id='poem_preface_11579_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_11579'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(950, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>铜乌</span>绕帝台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_11579'>帝台银阙距金塘，中间鹓鹭已成行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_11579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11579'>先过上苑传书信，暂下中州戏稻粱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_11579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11579'>虞人负缴来相及，齐客虚弓忽见伤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11579'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_11579", 11579, "Clauses/10/Comments/1")'>毛翎</span>频顿<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作憔悴）</span>飞无力，羽翮摧颓君不识。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11579'>惆怅惊思悲未已，裴回自怜中罔极。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11579'>传闻有鸟集朝阳，讵胜仙凫迩帝乡。<div id='poem_sentence_11_11579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_11579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_11579_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_11573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_11573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/11573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>羁卧山中</a><span class='authorDate'>（676年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_11573")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_11573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_11573'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_11573'>卧壑迷时代，行歌任死生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_11573'>红颜意气尽，白璧故交轻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_11573'>雪尽松帷暗，云开石路明。<div id='poem_sentence_4_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_11573'>夜伴饥鼯宿，朝随驯雉行。<div id='poem_sentence_5_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_11573'>度溪犹忆处，寻洞不知名。<div id='poem_sentence_7_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_11573'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_11573", 11573, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>扣<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作撞）</span>钟</span>鸣天鼓，烧香厌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_11573", 11573, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>地精</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_11573'>倘遇<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作过）</span>浮丘鹤，飘飖凌太清。<div id='poem_sentence_9_11573_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_11573'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_11573_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　居东龙门山.为来济作文集序。作品：《南阳公集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷6第335页。）</span><div id='poem_1363863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南阳公集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（677年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363863")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363863'>昔者龙蹲东鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363863_comment'></div>陈礼乐而救苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363863_comment'></div>虎据西秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363863_comment'></div>焚诗书以愚黔首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363863_comment'></div>通其变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363863_comment'></div>参天二地谓之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363863_comment'></div>合其机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363863_comment'></div>一阴一阳谓之圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363863_comment'></div>是以楚汉方斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363863_comment'></div>萧曹绛灌负长剑于此时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363863_comment'></div>袁曹已平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363863_comment'></div>徐陈应刘弄柔翰于当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363863_comment'></div>圣人方士之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363863_comment'></div>亦各异时而并宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363863_comment'></div>讴歌玉帛之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363863_comment'></div>何必同条而共贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363863_comment'></div>文质再而复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363863_comment'></div>殷周之损益足徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363863_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>骊翰</span>三而改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363863_comment'></div>虞夏之兴亡可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363863_comment'></div>美哉焕乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363863_comment'></div>斯文之功大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363863_comment'></div>自获麟绝笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363863_comment'></div>一千三四百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363863_comment'></div>游夏之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363863_comment'></div>时有荀卿孟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363863_comment'></div>屈宋之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363863_comment'></div>直至贾谊相如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363863_comment'></div>两班叙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363863_comment'></div>得邱明之风骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363863_comment'></div>二陆裁诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363863_comment'></div>含公干之奇伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363863_comment'></div>邺中新体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363863_comment'></div>共许音韵天成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363863_comment'></div>江左诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363863_comment'></div>咸好瑰姿艳发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363863_comment'></div>精博爽丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363863_comment'></div>颜延之急病于江鲍之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363863_comment'></div>疏散风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363863_comment'></div>谢宣城缓步于向刘之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1363863_comment'></div>北方重浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1363863_comment'></div>独卢黄门往往高飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1363863_comment'></div>南国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>轻清</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363863_comment'></div>惟庾中丞时时不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363863_comment'></div>嗟乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363863_comment'></div>古今之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363863_comment'></div>递相毁誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1363863_comment'></div>至有操我戈矛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1363863_comment'></div>启其墨守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1363863_comment'></div>三都既丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1363863_comment'></div>徵夏熟于上林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1363863_comment'></div>九辩已高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1363863_comment'></div>责春歌于下里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1363863_comment'></div>蹖駮之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1363863_comment'></div>纷然遂多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1363863_comment'></div>近日刘协文心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1363863_comment'></div>钟嵘诗评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1363863_comment'></div>异议蜂起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1363863_comment'></div>高谈不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1363863_comment'></div>人惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>西氏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1363863_comment'></div>空论拾翠之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1363863_comment'></div>质谢南金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1363863_comment'></div>徒辩荆蓬之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1363863_comment'></div>拔十得五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1363863_comment'></div>虽曰肩随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1363863_comment'></div>闻一知二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1363863_comment'></div>犹为臆说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1363863_comment'></div>佥曰未可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1363863_comment'></div>人称屡中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1363863_comment'></div>化鲁成鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1363863_comment'></div>曷云其远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1363863_comment'></div>非夫妙谐钟律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1363863_comment'></div>体会风骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1363863_comment'></div>笔有馀妍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1363863_comment'></div>思无停趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1363863_comment'></div>作龟作镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1363863_comment'></div>听歌曲而知亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1363863_comment'></div>为龙为光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1363863_comment'></div>观礼容而识大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1363863_comment'></div>齐鲁一变之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1363863_comment'></div>唐虞百代之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1363863_comment'></div>悬日月于胸怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1363863_comment'></div>挫风云于毫翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1363863_comment'></div>含今古之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1363863_comment'></div>扣宫徵之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1363863_comment'></div>细则出入无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1363863_comment'></div>粗则弥纶区宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1363863_comment'></div>逶迤绰约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1363863_comment'></div>如玉女之千娇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1363863_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>突兀</span>峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1363863_comment'></div>似灵龟之孤朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1363863_comment'></div>乘槎上汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1363863_comment'></div>谁问坳堂之浅深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1363863_comment'></div>荷戟入秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1363863_comment'></div>宁议长安之远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1363863_comment'></div>是非未定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1363863_comment'></div>曹子建皓首为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1363863_comment'></div>离合俱伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1363863_comment'></div>陆平叔终身流恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1363863_comment'></div>超然若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1363863_comment'></div>适可操刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1363863_comment'></div>自兹已降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1363863_comment'></div>徒劳举斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1363863_comment'></div>八病爰起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1363863_comment'></div>沈隐侯永作拘囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1363863_comment'></div>四声未分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1363863_comment'></div>梁武帝长为聋俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1363863_comment'></div>后生莫晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1363863_comment'></div>更恨文律烦苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1363863_comment'></div>知音者稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1363863_comment'></div>常恐词林交丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1363863_comment'></div>雅颂不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1363863_comment'></div>则后死者焉得而闻乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1363863_comment'></div>贞观年中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1363863_comment'></div>太宗外厌兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1363863_comment'></div>垂衣裳于万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1363863_comment'></div>舞干戚于两阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1363863_comment'></div>留思政涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1363863_comment'></div>内兴文事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1363863_comment'></div>虞李岑许之俦以文章进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1363863_comment'></div>王魏来褚之辈以材术显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1363863_comment'></div>咸能起自布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1363863_comment'></div>蔚为卿相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1363863_comment'></div>雍容侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1363863_comment'></div>朝夕献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1363863_comment'></div>我之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1363863_comment'></div>于斯为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1363863_comment'></div>虞博通万句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1363863_comment'></div>对问不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1363863_comment'></div>李长于五言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1363863_comment'></div>下笔无滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1363863_comment'></div>岑君<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_131_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>论诘</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_131_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/131/Comments/1")'>亹亹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1363863_comment'></div>听者忘疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1363863_comment'></div>许生章奏翩翩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1363863_comment'></div>谈之未易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1363863_comment'></div>王侍中政事精密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1363863_comment'></div>明达旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1363863_comment'></div>魏太师直气鲠辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1363863_comment'></div>兼包古义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1363863_comment'></div>来<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十二字）</span>褚河南风标特峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1363863_comment'></div>早锵声于册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1363863_comment'></div>变风变雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1363863_comment'></div>立体不拘于一涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1363863_comment'></div>既博既精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1363863_comment'></div>为学遍游于百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1363863_comment'></div>自豸冠指佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1363863_comment'></div>鸡树登贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1363863_comment'></div>内掌机密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1363863_comment'></div>外修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1363863_comment'></div>晨趋有暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1363863_comment'></div>持䌽笔于瑶轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1363863_comment'></div>夕拜多閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1363863_comment'></div>弄雕章于琴席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1363863_comment'></div>含毫顾盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1363863_comment'></div>汉家之城阙风烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1363863_comment'></div>逸韵纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1363863_comment'></div>秦地之林泉鱼鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1363863_comment'></div>黄山羽猎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1363863_comment'></div>几奏琼篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1363863_comment'></div>汾水楼船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1363863_comment'></div>参闻宝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1363863_comment'></div>南津吊屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1363863_comment'></div>去逐苍梧之云。<div id='poem_sentence_164_1363863_comment'></div>江湖廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1363863_comment'></div>造次不忒其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1363863_comment'></div>沙塞朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1363863_comment'></div>颠沛必归于汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1363863_comment'></div>是使名流俱至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1363863_comment'></div>兔翰阗门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1363863_comment'></div>爱客相寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1363863_comment'></div><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1363863_comment'></div>花欲白兮柳将菲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1363863_comment'></div>潎潎游鱼。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1363863_comment'></div>成三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1363863_comment'></div>早游西镐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1363863_comment'></div>及周史之阙文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1363863_comment'></div>晚卧东山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1363863_comment'></div>忆汉庭之遗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1363863_comment'></div>平津侯之宾馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1363863_comment'></div>马厩萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1363863_comment'></div>李司隶之仙舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1363863_comment'></div>龙门荒毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1363863_comment'></div>交交黄鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1363863_comment'></div>集于栩兮集于桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1363863_comment'></div>营营苍蝇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1363863_comment'></div>止于藩兮止于棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1363863_comment'></div>九原可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1363863_comment'></div>松有隧兮兔有埏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1363863_comment'></div>三湘不追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1363863_comment'></div>川无梁兮鸟无径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1363863_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_201_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/201/Comments/0")'>辍斤</span>之恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1363863_comment'></div>何独庄周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1363863_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_203_1363863", 1363863, "Clauses/203/Comments/0")'>闻笛</span>而悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1363863_comment'></div>宁惟向秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1363863_comment'></div>徒勤观海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1363863_comment'></div>未知渤潏之倪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1363863_comment'></div>永好谈天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1363863_comment'></div>莫究氤氲之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1363863_comment'></div>遂抽短翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1363863_comment'></div>为之序云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_210_1363863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=677&endYear=677')">677年</a>　居东龙门山.为贾言忠作乐府杂诗序。作品：《乐府诗杂序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷6第355页。）</span><div id='poem_1363864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐府杂诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（677年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363864")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363864'>闻夫歌以永言。庭坚有歌虞之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363864_comment'></div>颂以纪德。奚斯有颂鲁之篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363864_comment'></div>四始六义。存亡播矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363864_comment'></div>八音九阕。哀乐生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363864_comment'></div>是以叔誉闻诗。验同盟之成败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363864_comment'></div>延陵听乐。知列国之典彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363864_comment'></div>王泽竭而颂声寝。伯功衰而诗道缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363864_comment'></div>秦皇灭学。星琯千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363864_comment'></div>汉武崇文。市朝八变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363864_comment'></div>通儒作相。徵博士于诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363864_comment'></div>中使驱车。访<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>遗编</span>于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363864_comment'></div>发诏东观。缝掖成阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363864_comment'></div>献书南宫。丹铅踵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363864_comment'></div>王风国咏。共骊翰而升沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1363864_comment'></div>里颂途歌。随质文而沿革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1363864_comment'></div>以少卿长别。起高唱于河梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1363864_comment'></div>平子多愁。寄遥情于垄坂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1363864_comment'></div>南浦动关山之役。作者悲离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1363864_comment'></div>东京兴党锢之诛。词人哀怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1363864_comment'></div>后人鼓吹乐府。新声起于邺中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1363864_comment'></div>山水风云。逸韵生于江左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1363864_comment'></div>言古兴者多以西汉为宗。议今文者或用东朝为美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1363864_comment'></div>落梅芳树。共体千篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1363864_comment'></div>陇水巫山。殊名一意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1363864_comment'></div>亦犹负日于珍狐之下。沈萤于烛龙之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1363864_comment'></div>辛勤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>逐影</span>。更似悲狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1363864_comment'></div>罕见凿空。曾未先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1363864_comment'></div>潘陆颜谢。蹈迷津而不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1363864_comment'></div>任沈江刘。来乱辙而弥远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1363864_comment'></div>其有发挥新体。孤飞百代之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1363864_comment'></div>开凿古人。独步九流之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1363864_comment'></div>自我作古。粤在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1363864_comment'></div>乐府者。侍御史贾君之所作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1363864_comment'></div>君升堂入室。践<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>龟字</span>以长驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1363864_comment'></div>藏翼蓄鳞。展龙图以高视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1363864_comment'></div>林宗一见。许以王佐之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1363864_comment'></div>士季相看。知有公卿之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1363864_comment'></div>南国蛟龙之耀。下触词锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1363864_comment'></div>东家科斗之书。来游笔海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1363864_comment'></div>朝阳弄翮。即践中京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1363864_comment'></div>太行垂耳。先鸣上路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1363864_comment'></div>当赤县之枢钥。作高台之羽仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1363864_comment'></div>动息无隔于温仁。颠沛安由乎正义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1363864_comment'></div>玉阶覆奏。依然汲直之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1363864_comment'></div>铜术埋轮。先定雍门之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1363864_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>霜台</span>有暇。文律动于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1363864_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>绣服</span>无私。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>锦字</span>飞于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1363864_comment'></div>九成宫者。信天子之殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1363864_comment'></div>群山之一都也。五城既远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1363864_comment'></div>得昆阆于神京。三山已沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1363864_comment'></div>见蓬莱于古辅。紫楼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>金阁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1363864_comment'></div>雕石壁而镂群峰。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>碧甃</span>铜池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1363864_comment'></div>俯银津而横众壑。离宫地险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1363864_comment'></div>丹涧四周。徼道天回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1363864_comment'></div>翠屏千仞。卫尉寝蒙茸之署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1363864_comment'></div>将军无刁斗之警。中岩罢燠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1363864_comment'></div>飞霜为之夏凝。太谷生寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1363864_comment'></div>层淮以之秋冱。天子万乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1363864_comment'></div>驱凤辇于西郊。群公百僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1363864_comment'></div>扈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/118/Comments/0")'>龙轩</span>而北辅。春秋络绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1363864_comment'></div>冠盖满于青山。寒暑推移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1363864_comment'></div>旌节喧于黄道。夕宿鸡神之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1363864_comment'></div>朝登凤女之台。青鸟时飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1363864_comment'></div>白云无极。千年启圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1363864_comment'></div>邈同汾水之阳。七日期仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1363864_comment'></div>颇类缑山之曲。经过者徒知其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1363864_comment'></div>揄扬者未歌其事。恭闻首唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1363864_comment'></div>遂属洛阳之才。俯视前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1363864_comment'></div>将丽长安之道。平恩公当朝旧相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1363864_comment'></div>一顾增荣。亲行翰墨之林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1363864_comment'></div>先标唱和之雅。于是怀文之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1363864_comment'></div>莫不向风靡然。动麟阁之雕章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1363864_comment'></div>发鸿都之宝思。云飞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/145/Comments/0")'>绮札</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1363864_comment'></div>代郡接于苍梧。泉涌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>华篇</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1363864_comment'></div>岷波连于碣石。万殊斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1363864_comment'></div>千里不违。同晨风之鴥北林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1363864_comment'></div>似秋水之归东壑。洋洋盈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1363864_comment'></div>岂徒悬鲁之音。郁郁文哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1363864_comment'></div>非复从周之说。故可论诸典故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1363864_comment'></div>被以笙镛。爰有中山郎徐令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1363864_comment'></div>雅好著书。时称博物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1363864_comment'></div>探亡篇于古壁。徵逸于道人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1363864_comment'></div>撰而集之。命余为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1363864_comment'></div>时褫巾三蜀。归卧一邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1363864_comment'></div>散发书林。狂歌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_1363864", 1363864, "Clauses/169/Comments/0")'>学市</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1363864_comment'></div>虽江湖廊庙。宾庑萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1363864_comment'></div>绮季留侯。神交髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1363864_comment'></div>遂复驱偪幽忧之疾。经纬朝廷之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1363864_comment'></div>凡一百一篇。分为上下两卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1363864_comment'></div>俾夫舞雩周道。知小雅之欢娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1363864_comment'></div>击壤尧年。识太平之歌咏云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1363864_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1363864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=678&endYear=679')">678-679年</a>　居东龙门山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=680&endYear=680')">680年</a>　居东门山,病情加重,作《五悲文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷4第211页。祝氏笺注本作《五悲》）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
禹州（阳翟）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=681&endYear=681')">681年</a>　徙居具茨山,杨明府来访,作《杨明府过访诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷6第385页。）</span><div id='poem_1363867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1363867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1363867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨明府过访诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（681年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 初唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(13478, "初唐", "卢照邻", "poem_title_1363867")'>卢照邻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1363867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1363867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1363867'>夫清风动驾。谒阮籍于山阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1363867_comment'></div>素雪乘舟。访戴逵于江路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1363867_comment'></div>犹名高好事。迹标良史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1363867_comment'></div>未有莺临绮月。筵开许郭之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1363867_comment'></div>花聚繁星。门枉荀陈之驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1363867_comment'></div>泛烟光于紫潋。翻露色于丹滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1363867_comment'></div>亭皋一望。平芜千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1363867_comment'></div>萋萋芳草。童儿牧马之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1363867_comment'></div>亹亹朝川。野老休牛之塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1363867_comment'></div>钓台隐隐。先生之桑梓可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1363867_comment'></div>茨岭岩岩。隐士之风流尚在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1363867_comment'></div>岂使临邛樽酒。歌赋无声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1363867_comment'></div>彭泽琴书。田园寝咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1363867_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1363867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=681&endYear=681')">681年</a>　病笃,作《释疾文》三篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祝尚书《卢照邻集笺注》增订本上海古籍出版社2011年年版卷5第271页。卢照邻由东龙门山迁居阳翟具茨山,张志烈先生认为是因为由信佛转而宗道的缘故.参张谱217-220页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=682&endYear=682')">682年</a>　今年或明年,因病痛难耐,自投颍水而死。<br /></div>
